```sql
CREATE TABLE `tg_template_pack_tail_setting` (
  `id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键',
  `template_id` bigint DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '模板id',
  `name` varchar(64) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '名称',
  `description` varchar(256) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '描述',
  `tail_filter_json` json DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '打包长尾条件',
  `tail_fields_json` json DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '长尾处理字段',
  `deleted` int DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '是否删除',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB COMMENT='模板打包配置关联表';



alter table tg_application_info
    add pack_tail tinyint default 0 null comment '是否开启打包';

alter table tg_application_info
    add pack_tail_id int null comment '打包配置id';

alter table tg_application_info
    add pack_tail_name varchar(64) null comment '打包配置名称';

alter table tg_application_info
    modify pack_tail_id bigint null comment '打包配置id';

alter table tg_application_info
    change pack_tail pack_tail_switch tinyint default 0 null comment '是否开启打包';

alter table tg_template_pack_tail_setting
    modify description varchar(256) null comment '描述';


-- 模板改为：CMH_城市【通用】
update tg_asset_info set related_id = 114 where id in (211,221,222,223);
-- 模板改为：CMH_城市【通用】，关联模板资产为：CMH_城市【通用】
update tg_application_info set template_id = 114 , new_asset_id = 37 where template_id in (160,167,168,169);
-- 模板改为：CMH_城市【通用】，模板类型改为：通用
update tg_user_data_assets set template_id = 114 , template_type = 'customized' where template_id in (160,167,168,169);

-- 模板改为：CMH_城市_单品
update tg_asset_info set related_id = 100 where id in (201, 202);
-- 模板改为：CMH_城市_单品，关联模板资产为：CMH_城市_单品
update tg_application_info set template_id = 100 , new_asset_id = 29 where template_id in (152, 153);
-- 模板改为：CMH_城市_单品
update tg_user_data_assets set template_id = 100 where template_id in (152, 153);


CREATE TABLE `tg_application_form` (
  `id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'key',
    `application_id` varchar(255) NOT NULL COMMENT '当前关注的申请id',
  `application_no` varchar(255) NOT NULL COMMENT '需求编号',
  `apply_state` varchar(16) NOT NULL COMMENT '单状态',
  `apply_run_state` varchar(16) NOT NULL COMMENT '流程状态',
  `period` varchar(16) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '期数',
  `create_time` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `un_idx_no` (`application_no`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  COMMENT='需求单';

CREATE TABLE `tg_data_plan` (
  `id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'key',
  `biz_type` varchar(255) NOT NULL COMMENT '业务线',
  `day` date NOT NULL COMMENT '天',
  `holiday` tinyint NOT NULL COMMENT '节假日',
  `period` varchar(32) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '期数',
  `flow_process_type` varchar(16) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '类型',
    delay int comment '周期天数',
  `create_time` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
    updater bigint comment '更新人',
  `update_time` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  COMMENT='排期表';

```
